2025-12-22 16:24:17.305 +02:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (33ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[GroupName], [t].[RoleId], [t].[SecurityGroupId], [t].[Id], [t].[RoleName]
FROM [SecurityGroups] AS [s]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s0].[RoleId], [s0].[SecurityGroupId], [r].[Id], [r].[RoleName]
    FROM [SecurityGroupRoles] AS [s0]
    INNER JOIN [Roles] AS [r] ON [s0].[RoleId] = [r].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [s].[Id] = [t].[SecurityGroupId]
ORDER BY [s].[Id], [t].[RoleId], [t].[SecurityGroupId]
